\begin{Indent}{\bf Encoding/decoding problem index}\par
{\em General schema for encoding/decoding a problem index. Note that the index depends on the number of instances a suite is defined with (it should be called a suite-\/instance-\/depending index...). Also, while functions, instances and dimensions start from 1, function\+\_\+idx, instance\+\_\+idx and dimension\+\_\+idx as well as suite\+\_\+dep\+\_\+index start from 0!

Showing an example with 2 dimensions (2, 3), 5 instances (6, 7, 8, 9, 10) and 2 functions (1, 2)\+:

\begin{DoxyVerb}index | instance | function | dimension
------+----------+----------+-----------
    0 |        6 |        1 |         2
    1 |        7 |        1 |         2
    2 |        8 |        1 |         2
    3 |        9 |        1 |         2
    4 |       10 |        1 |         2
    5 |        6 |        2 |         2
    6 |        7 |        2 |         2
    7 |        8 |        2 |         2
    8 |        9 |        2 |         2
    9 |       10 |        2 |         2
   10 |        6 |        1 |         3
   11 |        7 |        1 |         3
   12 |        8 |        1 |         3
   13 |        9 |        1 |         3
   14 |       10 |        1 |         3
   15 |        6 |        2 |         2
   16 |        7 |        2 |         3
   17 |        8 |        2 |         3
   18 |        9 |        2 |         3
   19 |       10 |        2 |         3

index | instance_idx | function_idx | dimension_idx
------+--------------+--------------+---------------
    0 |            0 |            0 |             0
    1 |            1 |            0 |             0
    2 |            2 |            0 |             0
    3 |            3 |            0 |             0
    4 |            4 |            0 |             0
    5 |            0 |            1 |             0
    6 |            1 |            1 |             0
    7 |            2 |            1 |             0
    8 |            3 |            1 |             0
    9 |            4 |            1 |             0
   10 |            0 |            0 |             1
   11 |            1 |            0 |             1
   12 |            2 |            0 |             1
   13 |            3 |            0 |             1
   14 |            4 |            0 |             1
   15 |            0 |            1 |             1
   16 |            1 |            1 |             1
   17 |            2 |            1 |             1
   18 |            3 |            1 |             1
   19 |            4 |            1 |             1
\end{DoxyVerb}
 }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
size\+\_\+t \hyperlink{coco_8c_a56279a2384ad7255d0cc459c2d707284}{coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+encode\+\_\+problem\+\_\+index} (const \hyperlink{coco_8c_aa66be09e930304a945a3ff7dd06977f8}{coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t} $\ast$suite, const size\+\_\+t function\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t dimension\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t instance\+\_\+idx)

\end{Indent}

The maximum number of evaluations to trigger logging.

)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_aefefcc49b9024ff42d4487f3ff042f80}{}\label{coco_8c_aefefcc49b9024ff42d4487f3ff042f80}
avl\+\_\+rebalance\+: Rebalances the tree if one side becomes too heavy. This function assumes that both subtrees are A\+V\+L-\/trees with consistent data. The function has the additional side effect of recalculating the count of the tree at this node. It should be noted that at the return of this function, if a rebalance takes place, the top of this subtree is no longer going to be the same node. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!avl\+\_\+search\+\_\+rightish@{avl\+\_\+search\+\_\+rightish}}

Builds a coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t containing all the linear constraints by stacking them all. 

The constraints\textquotesingle{} gradients are randomly generated with distribution 10$\ast$$\ast$U\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} $\ast$ N\+\_\+i(0, I) $\ast$ 10$\ast$$\ast$\+U\+\_\+i\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]}, where U\mbox{[}a, b\mbox{]} is uniform in \mbox{[}a,b\mbox{]} and only U\+\_\+i is drawn for each constraint individually. The exception is the first constraint, whose gradient is given by 10$\ast$$\ast$U\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} $\ast$ (-\/feasible\+\_\+direction) $\ast$ 10$\ast$$\ast$\+U\+\_\+i\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]}.

Each constraint is built by calling the function \hyperlink{coco_8c_ac81a4a50f74a946211eb8c3283cf12ce}{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+single\+\_\+cons\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+problem\+\_\+allocate()}, which returns a coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t object that defines the constraint. The resulting coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t objects are then stacked together into one single coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t object that is returned by the function. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free@{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free}}
\index{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free@{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free(void $\ast$thing)}{c_linear_gradient_free(void *thing)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static void c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+free (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void $\ast$}]{thing}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a93de225812aeaab8e3e95b1fac29ce1c}{}\label{coco_8c_a93de225812aeaab8e3e95b1fac29ce1c}


Frees the data object. 

\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle@{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle}}
\index{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle@{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle(coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t $\ast$problem\+\_\+c, linear\+\_\+constraint\+\_\+data\+\_\+t $\ast$data\+\_\+c1)}{c_linear_shuffle(coco_problem_t *problem_c, linear_constraint_data_t *data_c1)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t} $\ast$ c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+shuffle (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{problem\+\_\+c, }
\item[{{\bf linear\+\_\+constraint\+\_\+data\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{data\+\_\+c1}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a3055d221d66acd60652987e0c914b9d1}{}\label{coco_8c_a3055d221d66acd60652987e0c914b9d1}


Exchange the first constraint for another one, if any, by exchanging their gradients. 

It picks a random constraint number different from one and runs through the stack of constraints until the chosen constraint is found. Then it extracts the gradient from it and exchange it for the first constraint\textquotesingle{}s. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+single\+\_\+cons\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+problem\+\_\+allocate@{c\+\_\+linear\+\_\+single\+\_\+cons\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+problem\+\_\+allocate}}

Creates a directory that has not existed before. 

If the given path does not yet exit, it is left as is, otherwise it is changed(!) by appending a number to it. If path already exists, path-\/001 will be tried. If this one exists as well, path-\/002 will be tried, and so on. If path-\/999 exists as well, an error is raised. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+current\+\_\+time\+\_\+get\+\_\+string@{coco\+\_\+current\+\_\+time\+\_\+get\+\_\+string}}

A function similar to coco\+\_\+info that prints only the given message without any prefix and without adding a new line. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+is\+\_\+feasible@{coco\+\_\+is\+\_\+feasible}}

Returns 1 if the point x is feasible, and 0 otherwise. 

Allows constraint\+\_\+values == N\+U\+LL, otherwise constraint\+\_\+values must be a valid double$\ast$ pointer and contains the g-\/values of x on \char`\"{}return\char`\"{}.

Any point x containing NaN or inf values is considered infeasible.

This function is (and should be) used internally only, and does not increase the counter of constraint function evaluations.

\hline
{\em x} & Decision vector. \\
\hline
{\em constraint\+\_\+values} & Vector of contraints values resulting from evaluation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Creates a platform-\/dependent path from the given strings. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The last argument must be N\+U\+LL. 

The first parameter must be able to accommodate path\+\_\+max\+\_\+length characters and the length of the joined path must not exceed path\+\_\+max\+\_\+length characters. 

Should work cross-\/platform.
\end{DoxyNote}
Usage examples\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item coco\+\_\+join\+\_\+path(base\+\_\+path, 100, folder1, folder2, folder3, N\+U\+L\+L) creates base\+\_\+path/folder1/folder2/folder3
\item coco\+\_\+join\+\_\+path(base\+\_\+path, 100, folder1, file\+\_\+name, N\+U\+L\+L) creates base\+\_\+path/folder1/file\+\_\+name 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em path} & The base path; it\textquotesingle{}s also where the joined path is stored to. \\
\hline
{\em path\+\_\+max\+\_\+length} & The maximum length of the path. \\
\hline
{\em ...} & Additional strings, must end with N\+U\+LL \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Feeds the solution to the bi-\/objective logger for logger output reconstruction purposes. 

Sets the number of evaluations, adds the objective vector to the archive and outputs information according to observer options (but does not output the archive).

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Vector y must point to a correctly sized allocated memory region and the given evaluation number must be larger than the existing one.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em problem} & The given C\+O\+CO problem. \\
\hline
{\em evaluation} & The number of evaluations. \\
\hline
{\em y} & The objective vector. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if archive was updated was done and 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+observer@{coco\+\_\+observer}}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{coco\+\_\+observer(const char $\ast$observer\+\_\+name, const char $\ast$options)}{coco_observer(const char *observer_name, const char *options)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+t} $\ast$ coco\+\_\+observer (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{observer\+\_\+name, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{observer\+\_\+options}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a363a2270ca7200445d21058e04433607}{}\label{coco_8c_a363a2270ca7200445d21058e04433607}


Constructs a C\+O\+CO observer. 

Currently, three observers are supported\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}bbob\char`\"{} is the observer for single-\/objective (both noisy and noiseless) problems with known optima, which creates $\ast$.info, $\ast$.dat, $\ast$.tdat and $\ast$.rdat files and logs the distance to the optimum.
\item \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj\char`\"{} is the observer for bi-\/objective problems, which creates $\ast$.info, $\ast$.dat and $\ast$.tdat files for the given indicators, as well as an archive folder with $\ast$.adat files containing nondominated solutions.
\item \char`\"{}toy\char`\"{} is a simple observer that logs when a target has been hit.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em observer\+\_\+name} & A string containing the name of the observer. Currently supported observer names are \char`\"{}bbob\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}toy\char`\"{}. Strings \char`\"{}no\+\_\+observer\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\char`\"{} or N\+U\+LL return N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em observer\+\_\+options} & A string of pairs \char`\"{}key\+: value\char`\"{} used to pass the options to the observer. Some observer options are general, while others are specific to some observers. Here we list only the general options, see observer\+\_\+bbob, observer\+\_\+biobj and observer\+\_\+toy for options of the specific observers.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}result\+\_\+folder\+: N\+A\+M\+E\char`\"{} determines the folder within the \char`\"{}exdata\char`\"{} folder into which the results will be output. If the folder with the given name already exists, first N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+001 will be tried, then N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+002 and so on. The default value is \char`\"{}default\char`\"{}.
\item \char`\"{}algorithm\+\_\+name\+: N\+A\+M\+E\char`\"{}, where N\+A\+ME is a short name of the algorithm that will be used in plots (no spaces are allowed). The default value is \char`\"{}\+A\+L\+G\char`\"{}.
\item \char`\"{}algorithm\+\_\+info\+: S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\char`\"{} stores the description of the algorithm. If it contains spaces, it must be surrounded by double quotes. The default value is \char`\"{}\char`\"{} (no description).
\item \char`\"{}number\+\_\+target\+\_\+triggers\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} defines the number of targets between each 10$\ast$$\ast$i and 10$\ast$$\ast$(i+1) (equally spaced in the logarithmic scale) that trigger logging. The default value is 100.
\item \char`\"{}target\+\_\+precision\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} defines the precision used for targets (there are no targets for abs(values) $<$ target\+\_\+precision). The default value is 1e-\/8.
\item \char`\"{}number\+\_\+evaluation\+\_\+triggers\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} defines the number of evaluations to be logged between each 10$\ast$$\ast$i and 10$\ast$$\ast$(i+1). The default value is 20.
\item \char`\"{}base\+\_\+evaluation\+\_\+triggers\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\char`\"{} defines the base evaluations used to produce an additional evaluation-\/based logging. The numbers of evaluations that trigger logging are every base\+\_\+evaluation $\ast$ dimension $\ast$ (10$\ast$$\ast$i). For example, if base\+\_\+evaluation\+\_\+triggers = \char`\"{}1,2,5\char`\"{}, the logger will be triggered by evaluations dim$\ast$1, dim$\ast$2, dim$\ast$5, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$1, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$2, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$5, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$1, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$2, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$5, ... The default value is \char`\"{}1,2,5\char`\"{}.
\item \char`\"{}precision\+\_\+x\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} defines the precision used when outputting variables and corresponds to the number of digits to be printed after the decimal point. The default value is 8.
\item \char`\"{}precision\+\_\+f\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} defines the precision used when outputting f values and corresponds to the number of digits to be printed after the decimal point. The default value is 15.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The constructed observer object or N\+U\+LL if observer\+\_\+name equals N\+U\+LL, \char`\"{}\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}no\+\_\+observer\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+allocate@{coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+allocate}}
\index{coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+allocate@{coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+allocate}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}

Creates and returns a structure containing information on triggers based on evaluation numbers. 

The numbers of evaluations that trigger logging are any of the two\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item every 10$\ast$$\ast$(exponent1/number\+\_\+of\+\_\+triggers) for exponent1 $>$= 0
\item every base\+\_\+evaluation $\ast$ dimension $\ast$ (10$\ast$$\ast$exponent2) for exponent2 $>$= 0
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The \hyperlink{structcoco__observer__evaluations__t}{coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+evaluations\+\_\+t} object instances need to be freed using the coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+evaluations\+\_\+free function!
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em base\+\_\+evaluations} & Evaluation numbers formatted as a string, which are used as the base to compute the second trigger. For example, if base\+\_\+evaluations = \char`\"{}1,2,5\char`\"{}, the logger will be triggered by evaluations dim$\ast$1, dim$\ast$2, dim$\ast$5, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$1, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$2, 10$\ast$dim$\ast$5, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$1, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$2, 100$\ast$dim$\ast$5, ... \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf coco\+\_\+observer\+\_\+evaluations\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{evaluations}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Returns 1 if any of the two triggers based on the number of evaluations equal 1 and 0 otherwise. 

The numbers of evaluations that trigger logging are any of the two\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item every 10$\ast$$\ast$(exponent1/number\+\_\+of\+\_\+triggers) for exponent1 $>$= 0
\item every base\+\_\+evaluation $\ast$ dimension $\ast$ (10$\ast$$\ast$exponent2) for exponent2 $>$= 0

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{coco\+\_\+options\+\_\+read\+\_\+values(const char $\ast$options, const char $\ast$name, char $\ast$pointer)}{coco_options_read_values(const char *options, const char *name, char *pointer)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static int coco\+\_\+options\+\_\+read\+\_\+values (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{options, }
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{pointer}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a4627c6e63ca741a5cb29a792f98adf52}{}\label{coco_8c_a4627c6e63ca741a5cb29a792f98adf52}


Reads (possibly delimited) values from options using the form \char`\"{}name1\+: value1,value2,value3 name2\+: value4\char`\"{}, i.\+e. reads all characters from the corresponding name up to the next alphabetic character or end of string, ignoring white-\/space characters. 

Formatting requirements\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item names have to start with alphabetic characters
\item values cannot include alphabetic characters
\item name and value need to be separated by a colon (spaces are optional)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of successful assignments. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Adds an observer to the given problem. 

Wraps the observer\textquotesingle{}s logger around the problem if the observer is not N\+U\+LL and invokes the initialization of this logger.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em problem} & The given C\+O\+CO problem. \\
\hline
{\em observer} & The C\+O\+CO observer, whose logger will wrap the problem.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The observed problem in the form of a new C\+O\+CO problem instance or the same problem if the observer is N\+U\+LL. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns the ID of the problem. 

The ID is guaranteed to contain only characters in the set \mbox{[}a-\/z0-\/9\+\_\+-\/\mbox{]}. It should therefore be safe to use it to construct filenames or other identifiers.

Each problem ID should be unique within each benchmark suite.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Do not modify the returned string! If you free the problem, the returned pointer becomes invalid. When in doubt, use \hyperlink{coco_8c_aa0c24d4a9eead3517bc1f1ca9be2f6ad}{coco\+\_\+strdup()} on the returned value. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Returns an initial solution, i.\+e. a feasible variable setting, to the problem. 

Copies problem-\/$>$initial\+\_\+solution into initial\+\_\+solution if not null, otherwise the center of the problem\textquotesingle{}s region of interest is the initial solution.

Returns the name of the problem. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Do not modify the returned string! If you free the problem, the returned pointer becomes invalid. When in doubt, use \hyperlink{coco_8c_aa0c24d4a9eead3517bc1f1ca9be2f6ad}{coco\+\_\+strdup()} on the returned value. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Removes an observer from the given problem. 

Frees the observer\textquotesingle{}s logger and returns the inner problem.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em problem} & The observed C\+O\+CO problem. \\
\hline
{\em observer} & The C\+O\+CO observer, whose logger was wrapping the problem.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The unobserved problem as a pointer to the inner problem or the same problem if the problem was not observed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item[{const double $\ast$}]{largest\+\_\+values\+\_\+of\+\_\+interest}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a0137a394b5a97e3bea88b95996db518f}{}\label{coco_8c_a0137a394b5a97e3bea88b95996db518f}


Allocates a problem constructed by stacking two C\+O\+CO problems. 

This is particularly useful for generating multi-\/objective problems, e.\+g. a bi-\/objective problem from two single-\/objective problems. The stacked problem must behave like a normal C\+O\+CO problem accepting the same input.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Regions of interest in the decision space must either agree or at least one of them must be N\+U\+LL. 

Best parameter becomes somewhat meaningless, but the nadir value make sense now. 
\end{DoxyNote}

A lagged Fibonacci random number generator. 

This generator is nice because it is reasonably small and directly generates double values. The chosen lags (607 and 273) lead to a generator with a period in excess of 2$^\wedge$607-\/1. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+new@{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+new}}
\index{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+new@{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+new}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}

Generates an approximately normal random number. 

Instead of using the (expensive) polar method, we may cheat and abuse the central limit theorem. The sum of 12 uniform random values has mean 6, variance 1 and is approximately normal. Subtract 6 and you get an approximately N(0, 1) random number. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform@{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform}}
\index{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform@{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform(coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+state\+\_\+t $\ast$state)}{coco_random_uniform(coco_random_state_t *state)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}double coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+uniform (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf coco\+\_\+random\+\_\+state\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{state}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{coco_8c_ab24243b4a151ff353436a243331e8a2a}{}\label{coco_8c_ab24243b4a151ff353436a243331e8a2a}

Creates and returns a string with removed characters between from and to. 

If you wish to remove characters from the beginning of the string, set from to \char`\"{}\char`\"{}. If you wish to remove characters until the end of the string, set to to \char`\"{}\char`\"{}.

The caller is responsible for freeing the allocated memory using \hyperlink{coco_8c_a8542ff7c23ec7a8e64487a50232db26f}{coco\+\_\+free\+\_\+memory()}. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+scale\+\_\+vector@{coco\+\_\+scale\+\_\+vector}}

Sets the C\+O\+CO log level to the given value and returns the previous value of the log level. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em log\+\_\+level} & Denotes the level of information given to the user through the standard output and error streams. Can take on the values\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}error\char`\"{} (only error messages are output),
\item \char`\"{}warning\char`\"{} (only error and warning messages are output),
\item \char`\"{}info\char`\"{} (only error, warning and info messages are output) and
\item \char`\"{}debug\char`\"{} (all messages are output).
\item \char`\"{}\char`\"{} does not set a new value The default value is info.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The previous coco\+\_\+log\+\_\+level value as an immutable string. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a1e00c4de35dff100917c3c49db7dcd2a}{}\label{coco_8c_a1e00c4de35dff100917c3c49db7dcd2a}


Returns the numbers defined by the ranges. 

Reads ranges from a string of positive ranges separated by commas. For example\+: \char`\"{}-\/3,5-\/6,8-\/\char`\"{}. Returns the numbers that are defined by the ranges if min and max are used as their extremes. If the ranges with open beginning/end are not allowed, use 0 as min/max. The returned string has an appended 0 to mark its end. A maximum of max\+\_\+count values is returned. If there is a problem with one of the ranges, the parsing stops and the current result is returned. The memory of the returned object needs to be freed by the caller. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split@{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split}}
\index{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split@{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split(const char $\ast$string, const char delimiter)}{coco_string_split(const char *string, const char delimiter)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static char$\ast$$\ast$ coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+split (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{string, }
\item[{const char}]{delimiter}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a4bc09b1e1f4505eb55d5191a3a204e07}{}\label{coco_8c_a4bc09b1e1f4505eb55d5191a3a204e07}


Splits a string based on the given delimiter. 

Returns a pointer to the resulting substrings with N\+U\+LL as the last one. The caller is responsible for freeing the allocated memory using \hyperlink{coco_8c_a8542ff7c23ec7a8e64487a50232db26f}{coco\+\_\+free\+\_\+memory()}. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+trim@{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+trim}}
\index{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+trim@{coco\+\_\+string\+\_\+trim}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a86aff0b1c28b4cf742bba04a8d6037ff}{}\label{coco_8c_a86aff0b1c28b4cf742bba04a8d6037ff}


Trims the given string (removes any leading and trailing spaces). 

If the string contains any leading spaces, the contents are shifted so that if it was dynamically allocated, it can be still freed on the returned pointer. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!coco\+\_\+suite@{coco\+\_\+suite}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

)}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a15a2cc9113dc64bba12180954a81fc98}{}\label{coco_8c_a15a2cc9113dc64bba12180954a81fc98}


Constructs a C\+O\+CO suite. 

Currently, six suites are supported\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}bbob\char`\"{} contains 24 \href{http://coco.lri.fr/downloads/download15.03/bbobdocfunctions.pdf}{\tt single-\/objective functions} in 6 dimensions (2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 40)
\item \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj\char`\"{} contains 55 \href{http://numbbo.github.io/coco-doc/bbob-biobj/functions}{\tt bi-\/objective functions} in 6 dimensions (2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 40)
\item \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj-\/ext\char`\"{} as an extension of \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj\char`\"{} contains 92 \href{http://numbbo.github.io/coco-doc/bbob-biobj/functions}{\tt bi-\/objective functions} in 6 dimensions (2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 40)
\item \char`\"{}bbob-\/largescale\char`\"{} contains 24 \href{http://coco.lri.fr/downloads/download15.03/bbobdocfunctions.pdf}{\tt single-\/objective functions} in 6 large dimensions (40, 80, 160, 320, 640, 1280)
\item \char`\"{}bbob-\/constrained\char`\"{} contains 48 linearly-\/constrained problems, which are combinations of 8 single objective functions with 6 different numbers of linear constraints (1, 2, 10, dimension/2, dimension-\/1, dimension+1), in 6 dimensions (2, 3, 5, 10, 20, 40).
\item \char`\"{}toy\char`\"{} contains 6 \href{http://coco.lri.fr/downloads/download15.03/bbobdocfunctions.pdf}{\tt single-\/objective functions} in 5 dimensions (2, 3, 5, 10, 20)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Only the suite\+\_\+name parameter needs to be non-\/empty. The suite\+\_\+instance and suite\+\_\+options can be \char`\"{}\char`\"{} or N\+U\+LL. In this case, default values are taken (default instances of a suite are those used in the last year and the suite is not filtered by default).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em suite\+\_\+name} & A string containing the name of the suite. Currently supported suite names are \char`\"{}bbob\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}bbob-\/biobj-\/ext\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}bbob-\/largescale\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}bbob-\/constrained\char`\"{}, and \char`\"{}toy\char`\"{}. \\
\hline
{\em suite\+\_\+instance} & A string used for defining the suite instances. Two ways are supported\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}year\+: Y\+E\+A\+R\char`\"{}, where Y\+E\+AR is the year of the B\+B\+OB workshop, includes the instances (to be) used in that year\textquotesingle{}s workshop;
\item \char`\"{}instances\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\char`\"{}, where V\+A\+L\+U\+ES are instance numbers from 1 on written as a comma-\/separated list or a range m-\/n. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em suite\+\_\+options} & A string of pairs \char`\"{}key\+: value\char`\"{} used to filter the suite (especially useful for parallelizing the experiments). Supported options\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}dimensions\+: L\+I\+S\+T\char`\"{}, where L\+I\+ST is the list of dimensions to keep in the suite (range-\/style syntax is not allowed here),
\item \char`\"{}dimension\+\_\+indices\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\char`\"{}, where V\+A\+L\+U\+ES is a list or a range of dimension indices (starting from 1) to keep in the suite, and
\item \char`\"{}function\+\_\+indices\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\char`\"{}, where V\+A\+L\+U\+ES is a list or a range of function indices (starting from 1) to keep in the suite, and
\item \char`\"{}instance\+\_\+indices\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\+S\char`\"{}, where V\+A\+L\+U\+ES is a list or a range of instance indices (starting from 1) to keep in the suite.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The constructed suite object. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a3670167c6247313ad7bf23a481356300}{}\label{coco_8c_a3670167c6247313ad7bf23a481356300}


Returns the next (observed) problem of the suite or N\+U\+LL if there is no next problem left. 

Iterates through the suite first by instances, then by functions and finally by dimensions. The instances/functions/dimensions that have been filtered out using the suite\+\_\+options of the coco\+\_\+suite function are skipped. Outputs some information regarding the current place in the iteration. The returned problem is wrapped with the observer. If the observer is N\+U\+LL, the returned problem is unobserved.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em suite} & The given suite. \\
\hline
{\em observer} & The observer used to wrap the problem. If N\+U\+LL, the problem is returned unobserved.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The next problem of the suite or N\+U\+LL if there is no next problem left. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns the number of problems in the given suite. 

The number of problems in the suite is computed as a product of the number of instances, number of functions and number of dimensions and therefore doesn\textquotesingle{}t account for any filtering done through the suite\+\_\+options parameter of the coco\+\_\+suite function.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em suite} & The given suite.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of problems in the suite. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns the first problem of the suite defined by function, dimension and instance numbers. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\+: While a suite can contain multiple problems with equal function, dimension and instance, this function always returns the first problem in the suite with the given function, dimension and instance values. If the given values don\textquotesingle{}t correspond to a problem, the function returns N\+U\+LL. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Initializes the biobjective logger. 

Copies all observer field values that are needed after initialization into logger field values for two reasons\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the observer is deleted before the suite, the observer is not available anymore when the logger is finalized.
\item This reduces function calls. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!logger\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+evaluate@{logger\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+evaluate}}

Updates the archive and buffer trees with the given node. 

Checks for domination and updates the archive tree and the values of the indicators if the given node is not weakly dominated by existing nodes in the archive tree. This is where the main computation of indicator values takes place.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the update was performed and 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{mo\+\_\+get\+\_\+dominance@{mo\+\_\+get\+\_\+dominance}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_ad132cc5f482428475aad0b8d29860463}{}\label{coco_8c_ad132cc5f482428475aad0b8d29860463}


Checks the dominance relation in the unconstrained minimization case between two normalized solutions in the objective space. 

If two values are closer together than mo\+\_\+precision, they are treated as equal.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if normalized\+\_\+y1 dominates normalized\+\_\+y2 ~\newline
 0 if normalized\+\_\+y1 and normalized\+\_\+y2 are non-\/dominated ~\newline
 -\/1 if normalized\+\_\+y2 dominates normalized\+\_\+y1 ~\newline
 -\/2 if normalized\+\_\+y1 is identical to normalized\+\_\+y2 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Creates a rounded normalized version of the given solution w.\+r.\+t. the given R\+OI. 

If the solution seems to be better than the extremes it is corrected (2 objectives are assumed). Initializes the bi-\/objective observer. 

Possible options\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}log\+\_\+nondominated\+: S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\char`\"{} determines how the nondominated solutions are handled. S\+T\+R\+I\+NG can take on the values \char`\"{}none\char`\"{} (don\textquotesingle{}t log nondominated solutions), \char`\"{}final\char`\"{} (log only the final nondominated solutions), \char`\"{}all\char`\"{} (log every solution that is nondominated at creation time) and \char`\"{}read\char`\"{} (the nondominated solutions are not logged, but are passed to the logger as input -\/ this is a functionality needed in pre-\/processing of the data). The default value is \char`\"{}all\char`\"{}.
\item \char`\"{}log\+\_\+decision\+\_\+variables\+: S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\char`\"{} determines whether the decision variables are to be logged in addition to the objective variables in the output of nondominated solutions. S\+T\+R\+I\+NG can take on the values \char`\"{}none\char`\"{} (don\textquotesingle{}t output decision variables), \char`\"{}low\+\_\+dim\char`\"{}(output decision variables only for dimensions lower or equal to 5) and \char`\"{}all\char`\"{} (output all decision variables). The default value is \char`\"{}low\+\_\+dim\char`\"{}.
\item \char`\"{}compute\+\_\+indicators\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} determines whether to compute and output performance indicators (1) or not (0). The default value is 1.
\item \char`\"{}produce\+\_\+all\+\_\+data\+: V\+A\+L\+U\+E\char`\"{} determines whether to produce all data required for the workshop. If set to 1, it overwrites some other options and is equivalent to setting \char`\"{}log\+\_\+nondominated\+: all\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}log\+\_\+decision\+\_\+variables\+: low\+\_\+dim\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}compute\+\_\+indicators\+: 1\char`\"{}. If set to 0, it does not change the values of the other options. The default value is 0. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!observer\+\_\+toy@{observer\+\_\+toy}}

\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance}}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance(coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t $\ast$suite, const size\+\_\+t instance, const size\+\_\+t instance1, const size\+\_\+t num\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+functions, const size\+\_\+t $\ast$bbob\+\_\+functions)}{suite_biobj_ext_get_new_instance(coco_suite_t *suite, const size_t instance, const size_t instance1, const size_t num_bbob_functions, const size_t *bbob_functions)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static size\+\_\+t suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{instance, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{instance1, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+functions, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{bbob\+\_\+functions}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a797897a0ccefa1deb79b1f8d7e6b7b14}{}\label{coco_8c_a797897a0ccefa1deb79b1f8d7e6b7b14}


Computes the instance number of the second problem/objective so that the resulting bi-\/objective problem has more than a single optimal solution. 

Starts by setting instance2 = instance1 + 1 and increases this number until an appropriate instance has been found (or until a maximum number of tries has been reached, in which case it throws a coco\+\_\+error). An appropriate instance is the one for which the resulting bi-\/objective problem (in any considered dimension) has the ideal and nadir points apart enough in the objective space and the extreme optimal points apart enough in the decision space. When the instance has been found, it is output through coco\+\_\+warning, so that the user can see it and eventually manually add it to suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+instances.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Copied from suite\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+biobj.\+c. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem}}
\index{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem(coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t $\ast$suite, const size\+\_\+t function\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t dimension\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t instance\+\_\+idx)}{suite_biobj_ext_get_problem(coco_suite_t *suite, const size_t function_idx, const size_t dimension_idx, const size_t instance_idx)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t}$\ast$ suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{suite, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{function\+\_\+idx, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{dimension\+\_\+idx, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{instance\+\_\+idx}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_adbd32293de4ac0e26321441baf89f9d1}{}\label{coco_8c_adbd32293de4ac0e26321441baf89f9d1}


Returns the problem from the bbob-\/biobj-\/ext suite that corresponds to the given parameters. 

Creates the bi-\/objective problem by constructing it from two single-\/objective problems from the bbob suite. If the invoked instance number is not in suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+instances, the function uses the following formula to construct a new appropriate instance\+:

problem1\+\_\+instance = 2 $\ast$ biobj\+\_\+instance + 1

problem2\+\_\+instance = problem1\+\_\+instance + 1

If needed, problem2\+\_\+instance is increased (see also the explanation of suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+ext\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em suite} & The C\+O\+CO suite. \\
\hline
{\em function\+\_\+idx} & Index of the function (starting from 0). \\
\hline
{\em dimension\+\_\+idx} & Index of the dimension (starting from 0). \\
\hline
{\em instance\+\_\+idx} & Index of the instance (starting from 0). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The problem that corresponds to the given parameters. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Copied from suite\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+biobj.\+c and extended. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance(coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t $\ast$suite, const size\+\_\+t instance, const size\+\_\+t instance1, const size\+\_\+t num\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+functions, const size\+\_\+t $\ast$bbob\+\_\+functions)}{suite_biobj_get_new_instance(coco_suite_t *suite, const size_t instance, const size_t instance1, const size_t num_bbob_functions, const size_t *bbob_functions)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static size\+\_\+t suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance (

\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{instance1, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+bbob\+\_\+functions, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{bbob\+\_\+functions}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_ae263020ff9af8b811166f20df592ca7a}{}\label{coco_8c_ae263020ff9af8b811166f20df592ca7a}


Computes the instance number of the second problem/objective so that the resulting bi-\/objective problem has more than a single optimal solution. 

Starts by setting instance2 = instance1 + 1 and increases this number until an appropriate instance has been found (or until a maximum number of tries has been reached, in which case it throws a coco\+\_\+error). An appropriate instance is the one for which the resulting bi-\/objective problem (in any considered dimension) has the ideal and nadir points apart enough in the objective space and the extreme optimal points apart enough in the decision space. When the instance has been found, it is output through coco\+\_\+warning, so that the user can see it and eventually manually add it to suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+instances. \index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem}}
\index{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem(coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t $\ast$suite, const size\+\_\+t function\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t dimension\+\_\+idx, const size\+\_\+t instance\+\_\+idx)}{suite_biobj_get_problem(coco_suite_t *suite, const size_t function_idx, const size_t dimension_idx, const size_t instance_idx)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}static {\bf coco\+\_\+problem\+\_\+t}$\ast$ suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+problem (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf coco\+\_\+suite\+\_\+t} $\ast$}]{suite, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{function\+\_\+idx, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{dimension\+\_\+idx, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{instance\+\_\+idx}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a44b8137e7dcba9d00fb1b99da7cea921}{}\label{coco_8c_a44b8137e7dcba9d00fb1b99da7cea921}


Returns the problem from the bbob-\/biobj suite that corresponds to the given parameters. 

Creates the bi-\/objective problem by constructing it from two single-\/objective problems from the bbob suite. If the invoked instance number is not in suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+instances, the function uses the following formula to construct a new appropriate instance\+:

problem1\+\_\+instance = 2 $\ast$ biobj\+\_\+instance + 1

problem2\+\_\+instance = problem1\+\_\+instance + 1

If needed, problem2\+\_\+instance is increased (see also the explanation of suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em suite} & The C\+O\+CO suite. \\
\hline
{\em function\+\_\+idx} & Index of the function (starting from 0). \\
\hline
{\em dimension\+\_\+idx} & Index of the dimension (starting from 0). \\
\hline
{\em instance\+\_\+idx} & Index of the instance (starting from 0). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The problem that corresponds to the given parameters. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{mo\+\_\+precision}{mo_precision}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}const double mo\+\_\+precision = 1e-\/13\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a51e1b3ffe514e06b45601b2f30d35414}{}\label{coco_8c_a51e1b3ffe514e06b45601b2f30d35414}


Precision used when comparing multi-\/objective solutions. 

Two solutions are considered equal in objective space when their normalized difference is smaller than mo\+\_\+precision.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
mo\+\_\+precision needs to be smaller than mo\+\_\+discretization 
\end{DoxyNote}
\index{coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}!suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp}}
\index{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp@{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp}!coco.\+c@{coco.\+c}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp}{suite_biobj_best_values_hyp}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}const char$\ast$ suite\+\_\+biobj\+\_\+best\+\_\+values\+\_\+hyp\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}\hypertarget{coco_8c_a9dc563cd895f0d35423d8766f2f2c7b6}{}\label{coco_8c_a9dc563cd895f0d35423d8766f2f2c7b6}


The best known hypervolume values for the bbob-\/biobj and bbob-\/biobj-\/ext suite problems. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Because this file is used for automatically retrieving the existing best hypervolume values for pre-\/processing purposes, its formatting should not be altered. This means that there must be exactly one string per line, the first string appearing on the next line after \char`\"{}static const char...\char`\"{} (no comments allowed in between). Nothing should be placed on the last line (line with \};). 
\end{DoxyNote}
